<div id="review_2084364237" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2084364237" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2084364237?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2084364237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer898042738842507589"><i>"What are you imagining? Your expression is filthy."<br/>"Strangling you. Bare hands." I can barely get the words out. I'm huskier than a phone-sex operator after a double shift.<br/>"So that's your kink." His eyes are going dark.</i><br/><br/>Oh, boy did I love those two!! XD<br/>I mean who wouldn’t enjoy reading banter like that? It was amazing and I couldn’t wait to read more about them! I swear their conversations were addicting and I loved the way Lucy narrated the story. I mean seriously! THAT GIRL!!! *lol* <br/><i>“I’m huski</i></span>
  <span id="freeText898042738842507589" style="display:none"><i>"What are you imagining? Your expression is filthy."<br />"Strangling you. Bare hands." I can barely get the words out. I'm huskier than a phone-sex operator after a double shift.<br />"So that's your kink." His eyes are going dark.</i><br /><br />Oh, boy did I love those two!! XD<br />I mean who wouldn’t enjoy reading banter like that? It was amazing and I couldn’t wait to read more about them! I swear their conversations were addicting and I loved the way Lucy narrated the story. I mean seriously! THAT GIRL!!! *lol* <br /><i>“I’m huskier than a phone-sex operator after a double shift”</i>!!!! Good grief!!! Haha! It were sentences like that which immediately caused me to love this book! XD Well, Lucinda’s narration <b>AND</b> the conversations between her and Josh!<br />They were like cat and mouse and I loved it!!! Actually I <b>
  <u>FREAKING LIVED FOR IT!</u>
</b>!!! &lt;333<br /><br />Also can we take a second and acknowledge that they were equal in every possible way! They both didn’t give each other an inch and this was refreshing! XD Finally two people that could not only give but also take! *lol* And Lucy’s password!!! I’m still not over it! Haha! I loved that Josh gave her the nickname “Shortcake” and I can’t believe that she didn’t get it!!! I mean OMG!!! How blind can you be?! XD The way they were at each other’s throat it’s no wonder the HR section was afraid of them. *lol*<br /><br /><i>“Tell me where to go, then."<br />"Go to hell." I start laughing again.<br />"So that's where you came from."</i><br /><br /><b>
  <u>BUT</u>
</b> <br />when the story finally took off!<br />When they eventually succumbed to their mutual attraction! <br />Hell, did it get steamy! Steamy enough to fog my imaginary reading glasses, I can assure you. ;-P<br /><br /><i>”There’s a fragility in this kiss I would have never expected. It’s the same as the knowledge that one day this memory will fade. He’s trying to make me remember this. It’s so bittersweet my heart begins to hurt.</i><br /><br />In short: <b>JOSH AND LUCY WERE AMAZING</b> and I even liked the sub-plot! XD I mean I couldn’t help but wonder why Josh was the way he was with his family but when I finally found out it all made sense! Poor Joshua! I wanted to hug and cuddle him! Okay, maybe I also wanted to touch his sexy muscles, but hey I’m just a girl! He sounded way too delicious to pass on such an opportunity. ;-P<br /><br />If there was one thing I didn’t like about <b>"The Hating Game”</b>, then it was the fact that the ending was so abrupt. Well, at least for me it was. I really would have liked to have a little more closure, but that’s just the romantic in me, so I guess others might be fine with the way it is. XD<br />And because I don’t want to spoil anything I’ll write my thoughts about the ending in a spoiler tag. Believe me it’s best for you. ;-P At least if you still want to read the book. Well, anyway:<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i>”He’s not a doctor. Deal with it.”<br />Anthony goggles at me.<br />“But I want you to know something. He could be, if he wanted to. He could be anything he fucking wanted to. Nothing is by mistake. Nothing is because he’s not good enough. It’s his choice.”</i><br /><br /><b>YOU GO GIRL!!!</b> I loved that Lucy defended Josh and told his father the things he never could! She was like a fierce lioness and I was soo damn proud of her!!! She kind of reminded me of myself when someone hurts my family and friends. *lol* Boy, I can be at least as fierce as her. Don’t let that nice smile deceive you, at night I fly either on a broom or a wyvern. ;-P<br /><br />Well anyway, back to the ending! XD This really was quite a surprise!!! I definitely didn’t expect it to go down like that. I mean I really thought one of them would win the interview and they’d find a way to deal with it. I never would have expected that Josh already thought about everything and even provided a solution! *lol* Knowing him I probably should have anticipated it though. Haha! <br />Still, I would have loved to see more of them together and I would have liked to have some sort of epilogue. It’s just my personal opinion though. *shrugs* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Conclusion:</b><br />A funny and fluffy contemporary is what I asked for and a funny and fluffy contemporary is exactly what I got! *lol*<br /><br />I can recommend <b>“The Hating Game”</b> to everyone who enjoys sassy banter with a hint of fluff and a dash of humour! If you want to dive into a sweet and short rom-com, this book certainly will be the right choice for you. ;-)</span>

No. I need a stronger word than love. <br/>Obsessed? Infatuated? Giddy? This is probably the best enemies to lovers story I have ever read.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488379284i/22107348._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lucy Hutton and Josh Templeman work</span>
  <span id="freeText7587302725360138498" style="display:none"><b> AMAZING NEWS!!!!!!!!! The Hating Game is coming to the big screen! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://deadline.com/2018/07/the-simpsons-david-mirkin-directing-the-hating-game-sally-thorne-1202433595/">https://deadline.com/2018/07/the-simp...</a> </b><br><br><b>MY DREAM CAST 😍</b><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/BDDnTct" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1532694590ra/26037105.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/Hgq5kaO" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492008943i/22472469._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't love this. No. I need a stronger word than love. <br>Obsessed? Infatuated? Giddy? Whatever, take your pick. <b>But Oh My Joshua, I am crazy for everything about this book.</b> The writing, the humor, the lust, the sexual tension, the emotion, the slow delicious burn. This is probably the best enemies to lovers story I have ever read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1488379284i/22107348._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucy Hutton and Josh Templeman work together at Gamin Publishing and Bexley Books and they have <b>hated each other</b> from the moment they met. They spend their days trying to out do and frustrate the other, play these ridiculous games (but I must say the Kissing Game was my favorite one), and their ultimate goal is to basically make the other cry. They are total opposites - Lucy is lovable, hysterical, and a people pleaser. Josh is a smart ass, grumpy, and cynical.<br><br><b>
  <i>"So painting your nails tonight, desperately alone?"<br> Lucky guess on his part?<br>"Yes. Masturbating and crying into your pillow, Doctor Joshua?" He looks at the top button of my shirt. <br>"Yes. And don't call me that."</i>
</b><br><br>Reading about these two fight? I was in TEARS. This was <u>HYSTERICAL.</u><br><br><b>
  <i>“What are you imagining? Your expression is filthy.”<br>“Strangling you. Bare hands.” I can barely get the words out. I’m huskier than a phone-sex operator after a double shift.</i>
</b><br><br>But reading about these two falling in love? My heart almost couldn't take it. <br><br><b>
  <i>“All I want to do is kiss you until I fall asleep. I want to slide in between your sheets, and find out what goes on inside your head, and underneath your clothes. I want to make a fool of myself over you.”<br><br>"The first smile Joshua's ever had in my presence is pressed against my lips."<br><br>"I love him so much it's like a thread piercing me. Punching holes. Dragging through. Stitching love into me. I'll never be able to untangle myself from this feeling. The color of love is surely this robin's-egg blue."</i>
</b><br><br>And my favorite line of all the lines:<br><br><b>
  <i>"I fucking love your red."</i>
</b><br><br>Joshua snuggling? I swoon. Joshua being romantic? I die. But when Joshua gets jealous? For the love of all that is holy, I can't deal. Joshua Templeman is a GOD and I love him unlike anyone or anything. He is mine. And I will fight you for him. The end. <br><br>There is no greater feeling than picking up a book and not expecting it to live up to the hype, only to find it does. IT SO DOES.<br><br>If I could give this book 6 million stars I would. If I could shout from every rooftop TO STOP WHAT YOU ARE DOING AND READ THIS RIGHT THIS SECOND I would. Do yourself a favor and read this phenomenal debut novel!<br><br><b>
  <i>"See,” he says into my mouth. “I don’t hate you, Lucy.”</i>

<div id="review_2314831557" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2314831557" />
    <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk"><img alt="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597641717p2/66224803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2314831557?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk" href="/user/show/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk">Jessi ♥️ H. Vojsk</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/27213238-the-hating-game">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66224803-jessi-h-vojsk?shelf=my-absolute-favorite">my-absolute-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2314831557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9032703310706279274"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450477822ra/17431313.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> “I have a theory. <br/>Hating someone feels disturbingly similar to being in love with them. <br/>I've had a lot of time to compare love and hate, and these are my observations.<br/>Love and hate are visceral.” </i> <br/><br/>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/>Sometimes (but rarely) when I finish a book, I think: <br/>I’d love to read this again. <br/>Like, right now.<br/>Is it too early to already start a reread? <br/>Yes? <br/>Well, but I want to. <br/>(My tbr-shelf is probably hating me right now)<br/>But... It was so freaking perfect. ♥️<br/>If you want to have a feel-nice-boo</span>
  <span id="freeText9032703310706279274" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450477822ra/17431313.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> “I have a theory. <br>Hating someone feels disturbingly similar to being in love with them. <br>I've had a lot of time to compare love and hate, and these are my observations.<br>Love and hate are visceral.” </i> <br><br>Story ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Sometimes (but rarely) when I finish a book, I think: <br>I’d love to read this again. <br>Like, right now.<br>Is it too early to already start a reread? <br>Yes? <br>Well, but I want to. <br>(My tbr-shelf is probably hating me right now)<br>But... It was so freaking perfect. ♥️<br>If you want to have a feel-nice-book then take this masterpiece and read it! I was smiling like a crazy maniac in the car/toilet/bus/bus station/ work/bedroom/ literally everywhere I took this book with me. <br>My boyfriend was not amused. (I neglected him... a bit while reading the book)<br>It’s about a boy and a girl who work with each other, both assistants and both have something in common: they hate each other. <br>But when things start to get chaotic Lucy isn’t so sure about her hate for Josh anymore. <br>It was so freakin lovely. Argh😍<br><br>Characters ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455435637ra/18100723.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If you’re searching for the absolute perfect man who you’ll love more than anyone, then stop looking because I found him and his name is Joshua Templeman. <br>He is gorgeous (obviously), funny, mature but still a little childish and he’s the absolute sweetest creature in the world. <br>He’ll send you flowers and make you compliments and he cares for you when you’re sick (even when you throw up like crazy). He just loves you with all his heart and it’s wonderful. <br>And he’s so intelligent and interesting! <br>I can’t get enough of him ♥️<br>Can someone get me a Josh Templeman please? I would love to have one myself 🙋🏻‍♀️<br>And Lucy... it was like I read this complete book from my own point of view. She was so so relatable. She was funny, a bit chaotic, super nice and such a sweetheart! <br>I loved her! ♥️ (not as much as Josh, but... still) <br>And Lucy’s dad is the absolute cutest dad ever. When Lucy was upset about Josh being mean he was calling him all the male names with a J, but not his real name. It was so funny and subtle protective. My heart melted for Lucy’s dad. <br>Can I have a father like this too? Thank you! <br><br>Relationships ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449086549ra/17231751.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh man, oh man. I feel like I was just pushed into a bottle of honey and when I broke surface I saw the rainbow-honeymoon-land with a lot of CUTENESS OVERLOAD! It was so freakin sweet and so funny I was smiling all the time. It made my heart warm and fluffy and my mood was sky high after reading this. <br>Josh and Lucy were such a funny, but still sweet couple. They cared for each other, protected each other even though they theoretically hated each other. But sometimes hate is just a mask and behind it there is shy innocent love ♥️<br><br>Writing style ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Well, well, well. This was a pretty awesome book with a great writing, awesome dialogues and characters. The fact that it was from the - oh so - relatable Lucy made it even more perfect. <br>If I’ll ever have a time when I’m sad, I’m probably going to read this 234 times in a row just to make myself happy again. <br>I hope that, if someone decides to read it, they’ll love lt as much as I did! 😘<br><br>First reread: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Me, while reading this book: <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444159586ra/16460711.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Still one of my favorite contemporary ♥️<br><br>Second reread: ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>If anyone asks me what my favorite book is - I will say this book, because every time I read it, I want to read it again and again and again.<br><br>German translation ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br>Oh, oh, oh. Now I know why I always read the originals in English. Translations are never as good as the original book. <br>Still, I loved the story. The characters. Everything. <br>Best book ever. (But only in English) </span>
  <a data-text-id="9032703310706279274" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2348489411" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2348489411" />
    <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey"><img alt="Chelsea Humphrey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585613513p2/47207032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2348489411?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea Humphrey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea Humphrey" href="/user/show/47207032-chelsea-humphrey">Chelsea Humphrey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/27213238-the-hating-game">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Chelsea by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/7382729-leigh-kramer">Leigh Kramer</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47207032-chelsea-humphrey?shelf=library">library</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2348489411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11088839764237949040">4.5 STARS<br/><br/>I've been seeing <i>The Hating Game</i> plastered across my Goodreads feed for well over a year now and avoided it solely due to my phase of being constantly disappointed by the majorly hyped books. I could just about slap myself silly for pushing this aside for so many months, because it was worth the hype and much more. While a little slow in the first few chapters, the story quickly takes off once the scene is set and I'm forced to admit something-<b>I have a serious obsession with love to hat</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11088839764237949040" style="display:none">4.5 STARS<br /><br />I've been seeing <i>The Hating Game</i> plastered across my Goodreads feed for well over a year now and avoided it solely due to my phase of being constantly disappointed by the majorly hyped books. I could just about slap myself silly for pushing this aside for so many months, because it was worth the hype and much more. While a little slow in the first few chapters, the story quickly takes off once the scene is set and I'm forced to admit something-<b>I have a serious obsession with love to hate tropes.</b> You heard me, I'm a walking, talking cliche and I'm not ashamed to admit it.<br /><br />There's not really much to go into regarding the plot here, as you pretty much get the details you need from the synopsis, but this book is just what it sounds like, a book all about two people concentrating on winning "The Hating Game", a past time where they spend every free moment plotting on how to sabotage one another. Lucy and Joshua work together for a publishing house that consists of a merger between two very different CEOs, and as Lucy and Josh find themselves up for the same promotion, they are forced to declare all out war, and as the tension builds they discover that maybe they have been wrong about each other all along.<br /><br />I've seen some reviews that claim they would have enjoyed this more if the "hating" stage had lasted longer, but IMO it was the perfect length of time. The fact that this book wasn't just sexy, but also hilarious? That was a huge bonus. Thorne's writing made me feel like I'd found a bosom buddy in my bizarre sense of humor. I also didn't realize this book would be more than a piece of fluffy goodness... You know, the ones that are wholly enjoyable but completely forgettable? Not this one. I was completely taken with the fact that the author chose to have her characters wrestle with some below surface, realistic issues. By the end of this book I was ready to fight anyone who hurt my precious pumpkin Joshua Templeman. <br /><br /><i>The Hating Game</i> was a juicy delight; the characters were larger than life and the plot was unique while maintaining a semblance of comfort and reliability. If you have been living under a rock (like me) and haven't managed to move this up your TBR yet, go ahead and block out your weekend to devour this baby. I'm so glad I've decided to focus on expanding my reading to cover a wider variety of genres this year; I can finally stop kicking myself for missing this one and join in the fandom awaiting Thorne's next novel. Highly recommended for a feel good, rip-roaring time! <br /><br /><i>Buddy read with my partner in crime <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/20224869-sam-clues-and-reviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Sam @ CluesAndReviews</a> </i> &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="11088839764237949040" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1749087460" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12130193607786893110">OMG! This book had me in stitches! It was hilarious. I listened to the audiobook version and spent the day smiling like a loon while everyone in my house wondered what was so entertaining about doing the laundry. <br/><br/>The story revolves around Lucy Hutton and Joshua Templeman, two executive assistants forced together when rival publishing companies merge, making their respective bosses co-CEOs. They spend their days antagonizing each other and verbally sparring. I laughed my ass off listening to thei</span>
  <span id="freeText12130193607786893110" style="display:none">OMG! This book had me in stitches! It was hilarious. I listened to the audiobook version and spent the day smiling like a loon while everyone in my house wondered what was so entertaining about doing the laundry. <br /><br />The story revolves around Lucy Hutton and Joshua Templeman, two executive assistants forced together when rival publishing companies merge, making their respective bosses co-CEOs. They spend their days antagonizing each other and verbally sparring. I laughed my ass off listening to their back and forth, passive aggressive banter. Right from the start, they had me completely hooked.<br /><br />As the story progresses, the attraction between the two becomes more undeniable. I mean, I always knew that it was there, but waiting for it to evolve in the story was killer. These two definitely had a love-hate relationship and I knew that they would be explosive when they finally got on the same page.<br /><br />I have to say that I was not disappointed, at all. The author definitely keeps you waiting, but it is sooo worth it. I loved seeing the softer, more vulnerable side of these characters as their relationship grew increasingly intimate.<br /><br />If you're in the mood for a light-hearted, romantic comedy, I highly recommend 'The Hating Game'. It is cute, sweet and laugh-out-loud funny. The narration was wonderful as well. This was a great change of pace for me and one that I'll probably revisit in the future.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> </span>

    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39722464-arini?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2079594934" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7369130472732679921"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1583075823i/29042592._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>📚 <b>1st Reading, August 2017 — 5 Stars<br/>🎧 2nd Reading, February 2020 — 5 Stars<br/>🎧 3rd Reading, September 2020 — 5 Stars</b><br/><br/>My fangirling might make you cringe, but please don’t rain on my parade. <b>I LOVE THIS BOOK SO MUCH I COULD CRY.</b> And I’m shamelessly admitting that I literally did. The last chapter was so sweet I smiled so big my cheeks hurt. I didn’t mean to get all corny and mushy, but <b>I JUST FEEL LIKE MY HEART IS SO FULL AND I’M ABOUT TO PUKE RAINBOWS</b>.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441147600ra/16068907.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>How is it fair that in all the history of my nin</span>
  <span id="freeText7369130472732679921" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1583075823i/29042592._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>📚 <b>1st Reading, August 2017 — 5 Stars<br>🎧 2nd Reading, February 2020 — 5 Stars<br>🎧 3rd Reading, September 2020 — 5 Stars</b><br><br>My fangirling might make you cringe, but please don’t rain on my parade. <b>I LOVE THIS BOOK SO MUCH I COULD CRY.</b> And I’m shamelessly admitting that I literally did. The last chapter was so sweet I smiled so big my cheeks hurt. I didn’t mean to get all corny and mushy, but <b>I JUST FEEL LIKE MY HEART IS SO FULL AND I’M ABOUT TO PUKE RAINBOWS</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441147600ra/16068907.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How is it fair that in all the history of my nine to five jobs I’ve never had a co-worker like <b>JOSHUA TEMPLEMAN</b>?<br><br>Granted I’d just graduated so I barely have any career to speak of. I would also probably die from stress and mortification if I had to deal with someone who constantly reprimanded my work ethic and teased me to the point of madness on a daily basis like Josh did Lucy.<br><br>But I digress.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I want to make a fool of myself over you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I LOVE big, tall, grouchy, intimidating, perceptive, neat freak, and smart as a whip <b>JOSH</b>. He’s almost never nice, but who wants nice anyway? (LOL I’m going to get trolled over this. But no ladies, please find yourself a nice guy.) Anyway, it doesn’t matter bcs his heart is in the right place. He’s misunderstood and a little shy. He’s actually a giant softie.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ll never be able to untangle myself from this feeling. The color of love is surely this robin’s-egg blue.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I freaking ADORE <b>Lucy</b>, Heiress of the Sky Diamond Strawberries Dynasty. Lara Croft Lucinda is my favorite. She can be a bit of a pushover, but she kicks <i>ass</i> in her five inch heels and with her Flamethrower red lips. She has the most wonderful relationship with her parents and I’m just all here for it.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“What are you imagining? Your expression is filthy.”<br>“Strangling you. Bare hands.”<br>“So that’s your kink.”<br>“Only where you’re concerned.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>These two are so ADORKABLE together. Their banter, their stupid fights and games, their flirting, gah . . . their dynamics is everything! Being in their presence is so addictive. I couldn’t wipe the grin off my face even if I tried. They are so much fun to hang around I never wanted this book to end!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511461074ra/24515850.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To be honest, the audiobook isn’t all that great. The narrator doesn’t vocalize Lucy and Josh’s voices distinctly that sometimes it was lost on me who was speaking what. However, I also think I wouldn’t have gotten this emotional over this book had I just read it conventionally. Anyhow, I still consider this one of my best audiobook experiences.<br><br>I’m normally not into office romances considering guys in corporate businesses are not the type of heroes I want to read about. (No offense!) But this book ticks all my boxes. I’m fairly certain I won’t ever get sick of rereading this. You can say whatever you want, but <b>THIS BOOK IS A MASTERPIECE</b>. I believe that anyone who hasn’t read this is doing themselves a disservice. I’m so excited for the film!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7369130472732679921" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1661433198963209119">Re-read #3 (4/14/2020) Reread again because it’s my birthday and I’d rather spend it with no one but Joshua and Lucy. There’s no explainable reason why I love this book so much. It’s just that when all goes down, I can always count on this book to make it all okay. This book make me so freakin happy!!<br/><br/>Re-read #2 (9/2/2019) Hands down the best rom-com book I’ve ever read!! This book brings joy to my life. <br/>I LOVE IT SO FREAKIN MUCH!! <br/><br/><b>5 shortcake stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551558457i/27144675._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <b>”I should mention that the ultimate aim of all</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1661433198963209119" style="display:none">Re-read #3 (4/14/2020) Reread again because it’s my birthday and I’d rather spend it with no one but Joshua and Lucy. There’s no explainable reason why I love this book so much. It’s just that when all goes down, I can always count on this book to make it all okay. This book make me so freakin happy!!<br><br>Re-read #2 (9/2/2019) Hands down the best rom-com book I’ve ever read!! This book brings joy to my life. <br>I LOVE IT SO FREAKIN MUCH!! <br><br><b>5 shortcake stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1551558457i/27144675._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <b>”I should mention that the ultimate aim of all our games is to make the other smile, or cry. It’s something like that. I’ll know when I win.”</b><br><br>Sally Thorne, you’re amazing! The hating game was a really beautiful book. One of the best enemies to lovers books. I was smiling through the whole book. God! My face hurts!<br><br>Lucy Hutton and Joshua Templeman has been playing the hating game, in addition to many other games I’ve never known excited until I read this book, since Gamin Publishing and Bexley Books merged to avoid financial ruin. Both are executive assistants to the owners of the publishing house. They both share an office, a competitive spirit, and mutual hate.<br>Other than that, those characters are totally different. Lucy is the nice, funny, and lovable. While josh is grumpy, cynical and made everyone tremble. no one can provoke josh like Lucy and no one can annoy the hell out of Lucy like josh. The best thing is that they were so compatible they both could give it back as good as they can take it. I absolutely loved them!!<br><br> <b>”Tell me where to go, then."<br> “Go to hell." I start laughing again.<br> “So that's where you came from."</b><br><br>Things start to get worse (or better) when they found out that one of them would be promoted to be the other’s boss. Their competition went to another new level. Although their relation seemed to take another route after one mind blowing kiss. <br><br><b>”When you get so little of someone, you take what you can get.”</b><br><br>The book was perfect. It was so entertaining, hilarious, adorable, and full of sassy banters. I can’t believe that this was a debut novel. It’s just really good! It’s more than just a fun read, there were also a softer, more vulnerable side to the characters that made the story really good. Then you find yourself in love! With the characters, the dialogue, the story, the writing and definitely with the author.<br>Lucy and Joshua might be my favorite nemesis ever! <br><br> <b>”Shortcake”<br> “Stop calling me shortcake”<br> “Watching you pretend to hate that nickname is the best part of my day.”</b><br><br><b>song recommendation:</b><br>Papercuts by IIIy (ft. Vera blue)</span>

<div id="review_2099191444" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2099191444" />
    <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson"><img alt="Whitney Atkinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550868411p2/14457130.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2099191444?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Whitney Atkinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Whitney Atkinson" href="/user/show/14457130-whitney-atkinson">Whitney Atkinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=favs-of-2018">favs-of-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=smutty">smutty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=healthy-romance">healthy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=superior-enemies-to-lovers">superior-enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2099191444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9437817672537666302">4.5 Stars<br/><br/>Every book needs to take notes from the way this romance is written. It's exactly the type of detailing that I crave in books like this and i'm SO thrilled I finally got the chance to read this and add to my list of new favorites, even though it wasn't perfect.<br/><br/>The beginning of this book needs to be fleshed out a lot more. We’re told that Lucy haaates Josh, but there’s nothing substantial to back that up, and she kinda just tells the reader HE’S HORRIBLE AND ANNOYING AND I’VE HATED HIM F</span>
  <span id="freeText9437817672537666302" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br />Every book needs to take notes from the way this romance is written. It's exactly the type of detailing that I crave in books like this and i'm SO thrilled I finally got the chance to read this and add to my list of new favorites, even though it wasn't perfect.<br /><br />The beginning of this book needs to be fleshed out a lot more. We’re told that Lucy haaates Josh, but there’s nothing substantial to back that up, and she kinda just tells the reader HE’S HORRIBLE AND ANNOYING AND I’VE HATED HIM FOR YEARS AND HE’S THE WORST but we never actually see anything he does that’s bad or annoying, he literally just sits at his desk.<br /><br />Usually when books try to be quirky and humorous, I’m gagging and it and rolling my eyes. This is the first book where it actually, truly worked and I was laughing out loud, which is such a rare phenomenon that I would almost argue it only ever happens in like 3 books per year, and 2 of those are shatter me rereads. The writing style is something I usually hate, but the author made it work, so bravo. The only issue that arose with the writing style was that the quirky dialogue and inner monologue began to have lots of micro-issues, which aren’t bad on their own, but for me to stop every few pages and think “oh, that’s distasteful,” it weighed down my reading experience. This mainly lay in Lucy's fatphobia and constantly calling one of her bosses Fat Little Dick, but there were some other comments that used the r-word or other distasteful jokes.<br /><br />Additionally, sometimes Lucy and the way she thought and spoke were a little <i>too</i> childish. I feel like no adults would behave like the way she did sometimes, and I certainly understand how people could pick this up, read 5 pages of it, go “ugh,” and put it back down. There’s an inherent quality of hyperbole to the story just because of the way it’s written and with Lucy’s mind/reactions to things. A lot of times it comes off as cute, but other times, it's weirdly creepy Sometimes it feels like she’s infantilized just a little with over-exaggerated descriptions of how tiny she is and how childish her brain operates at times, but it never dumbed down the story too much for me. Overall, I really loved her as a main character and didn't think her character was too gimmicky or stereotypical, but she did feel slightly at arm's length just because she had that childish quality to her.<br /><br />Going along with the characters being immature, there was a weird, over-protective vibe within the book’s love triangle that rubbed me the wrong way. Two men were obviously into Lucy, but they used her like an object to deflect their possessiveness of her and it was dehumanizing to see how angry one would be when she spent time with the other. The masculine “NO SHE’S MINE” energy was just unbearable in this one, but there was an apology and a discussion about it, so I'm letting it slide.<br /><br />But the bottom line: I’m a slut for soft characters, and Josh was soft from the beginning. I actually teared up the first time Josh hurt Lucy’s feelings and she caught his eyebrows creasing in concern. Like… small gestures like that just <b>Get</b> me. Even though the taunting and the constant watching could be creepy, small moments like those slipped through the cracks and I was so grateful. Throughout the book, I was just so impressed by the softness of gestures. I really can’t expound enough how much of a sucker I am for tiny details and descriptions like the tendons in someone’s hands or the feel of fingertips on skin and other minuscule images, but this had so many, the story felt tangible. It’s my absolute favorite kind of story telling and what I look for (or hope to find) in every book I read. If this author wrote a more serious, dark fantasy using those same kinds of descriptions, it would probably be my new favorite book of all time.<br /><br />Usually when I read romance books I just tolerate the characters and the romance scenes are satisfactory at best, but this book had me crying and smiling and texting mahana reactions every 5 seconds. I've never been so attached to two character's love story, and it was paced in a way that was so addicting. Like I'm not kidding, I used to say Easy by Tammara Webber should be a blueprint for how all romance should be written, but this might replace it. I love the angst and slow build and the genuine connection. It was so refreshing to fall in love with characters rather than feel like I'm reading a regurgitation of every romantic story I've ever consumed. <br /><br />I highly applaud this book despite its flaws, and I definitely recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9437817672537666302" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2222015727" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2222015727" />
    <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance"><img alt="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513125058p2/68538597.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2222015727?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance">❄️BooksofRadiance❄️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2222015727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9415630861232098546">So I finally read the romance book that took GR and other book communities by storm and... I liked it? It was okay. And cute. <br/>I wouldn’t say I fell madly in love with it like most people did but it was fun. That’s about it. <br/><br/>Let me preface this by saying that I wanted to (really) love it. I truly and genuinely did but the fact of the matter is that fluffy contemporary romance novels just aren’t my thing. I tried. <br/>If given the choice, I’d always go for plot-driven books-at least for the most part-</span>
  <span id="freeText9415630861232098546" style="display:none">So I finally read the romance book that took GR and other book communities by storm and... I liked it? It was okay. And cute. <br />I wouldn’t say I fell madly in love with it like most people did but it was fun. That’s about it. <br /><br />Let me preface this by saying that I wanted to (really) love it. I truly and genuinely did but the fact of the matter is that fluffy contemporary romance novels just aren’t my thing. I tried. <br />If given the choice, I’d always go for plot-driven books-at least for the most part-, so I found this a tad boring as there was nothing to look forward to. Nothing to get my juices flowing, get my pulses racing or have my heart fluttering. <br /><br />Personally speaking, and this is purely a personal taste, I get painfully and utterly bored with books where the entirety of the plot revolves around two people and their inevitable end together. Where you know the end just by reading the blurb. <br />There’s no anticipation, no surprises, no ‘twists’, just two destined-to-end-up-together people going back and forth trying to find reasons why they should or should not be together. Eh. <br /><br /><b>What I liked:</b><br /><br />Lucie and Josh. <br />Normally, I hate self deprecating characters. It’s not cute, it’s not “relatable”; it’s just annoying. They just come off plain insincere but Lucie was genuinely adorable and I was seriously surprised by how much I loved her ‘cause I went in afraid that I wouldn’t. <br />Josh was (almost) everything a man should be. Only, he was too... perfect. <br /><br /><b>What I didn’t like:</b><br /><br />That Josh was too perfect. I get trying to lure readers into loving him and going all ga ga over him but this was a few steps too far for my liking. <br />I didn’t like how Lucie worshiped him. I say worship because everything he said and did, everything that was related to him was... that’s right, perfect. Too much for my taste. <br /><br />All in all, it was fun.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9415630861232098546" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1745334967" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1745334967" />
    <a title="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog"><img alt="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484605631p2/44673856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1745334967?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦" href="/user/show/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog">Maria✦❋Steamy Reads Blog❋✦</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=office-romance">office-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44673856-maria-steamy-reads-blog?shelf=romcoms">romcoms</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1745334967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7526977208349048422"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466194304i/19451974.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474158984i/20562421._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want to know what's going on in your brain. I want to juice your head like a lemon."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473869396i/20525269.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>➦This is Sally Thorne's <b>debut novel</b> and I have to say - <b>job well done!</b> I love romcoms and this one certainly hit the spot. A book about <b>two co-workers</b> battling it out in the office. You see, there is an opening for a job which they both want. Let the games begin.<br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"-What are you imagining? Your expression is filthy."<br/><br/>"-Stangling you. Bare hands."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>➦<b>Lucy</b> is a sweetheart and a <b>people pleaser.</b> </span>
  <span id="freeText7526977208349048422" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466194304i/19451974.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474158984i/20562421._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I want to know what's going on in your brain. I want to juice your head like a lemon."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473869396i/20525269.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>➦This is Sally Thorne's <b>debut novel</b> and I have to say - <b>job well done!</b> I love romcoms and this one certainly hit the spot. A book about <b>two co-workers</b> battling it out in the office. You see, there is an opening for a job which they both want. Let the games begin.<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"-What are you imagining? Your expression is filthy."<br><br>"-Stangling you. Bare hands."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>➦<b>Lucy</b> is a sweetheart and a <b>people pleaser.</b> So why is it so hard for her to get along with <b>Josh?</b> Well, because he is a major <b>asshole.</b> Yep. Perhaps, he's <b>compensating for something?</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394224147ra/8824486.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>➦Will Lucy be able see the <b>gentle man</b> beneath the brute masculine facade? <br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474158984i/20562422.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>❤The novel is written from <b>Lucy's POV</b> and I loved her thoughts - they were entertaining and on point. The banter between her and Josh was great - <b>I was never bored.</b> The chemistry and anticipation was there and the <b>slow burn was delicious.</b> <br><br>❤Now, personally, I'm a fan of slow burn but I see how some friends might get impatient with it. :) This novel is a bit <b>low on steam</b>, you won't find phrases like <b>"he stuck his cock in my vagina and pumped hard."</b> It will be along the lines of <b>"he moved inside me with a delicious rhythm."</b> It was tastefully done, I had no problem with it. Some parts were rather hot and gave me <b>goosebumps.</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"-What's with the weird eyes? Relax."<br><br>"-I was thinking about how big you are."<br><br>"-I'll fit you just right."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392746989ra/8604565.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She wasn't talking about his <b>male appendage</b>, by the way. The man is <b>T-A-L-L. </b><br><br>➦One thing I found lacking was <b>the ending.</b> I felt it was a bit <b>abrupt</b> and it just felt like all the dominoes fell back in place in a matter of minutes. That's just my opinion. Perhaps I was so in love with the characters that <b>I didn't want the novel to end.</b> Epilogue would have satisfied me, I think. Heh, I'm just being picky. :)<br><br>➦Recommended for those who love <b>romantic comedies, office romances, love-hate relationships</b> and <b>asshole alphas.</b> I'll be on the look-out for more of Sally Thorne's books. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473869396i/20525269.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525702.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525703.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.steamyreads.net" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525705.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2114037978" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14817882676997756038">I devoured this book in a day!! I couldn’t put it down!! The chemistry was sooooo hot 🔥🔥🔥 Lucy is well liked by everyone in the office, except for Josh. The hatred they have for each other, the friction, the angst, was just so frustratingly good! When a promotion becomes available, these two rivals are both in it to win it. I don’t want to give anything away. 😉 I will caution that this is rated R and may not be suitable for my more wholesome and/or younger friends. 😍❤️</span>

<div id="review_1747734782" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1747734782" />
    <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog"><img alt="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465210954p2/41356020.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1747734782?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog" href="/user/show/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog">Nissa | Of Pens and Pages Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=adult-romance">adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=hate-to-love">hate-to-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41356020-nissa-of-pens-and-pages-book-blog?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1747734782" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12618860543148069517"><a href='http://www.ofpensandpages.com/2016/09/review-hating-game-by-sally-thorne.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Review at Of Pens and Pages.</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478786135i/21111629._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>
  <b>Reasons why I loved The Hating Game </b>
</u><br/><br/>1. Lucy Hutton<br/>2. Josh Templeman<br/>3. The banter<br/>4. The chemistry<br/>5. SLOW.BURN.<br/>6. Matchbox cars<br/>7. Smurfs<br/>8. White, off-white stripe, cream, pale yellow, mustard, baby blue, robin's egg blue, dove-gray, navy, and black business shirts<br/>9. CUDDLING<br/>10. Hate to love<br/><br/>I devoured this book. <i>Completely devoured it.</i> I was looking for a slow-burn, hate to love office romance, and this was it. I am so happy right now, you guys. I'm literally grinni</span>
  <span id="freeText12618860543148069517" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.ofpensandpages.com/2016/09/review-hating-game-by-sally-thorne.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Review at Of Pens and Pages.</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478786135i/21111629._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>Reasons why I loved The Hating Game </b>
</u><br><br>1. Lucy Hutton<br>2. Josh Templeman<br>3. The banter<br>4. The chemistry<br>5. SLOW.BURN.<br>6. Matchbox cars<br>7. Smurfs<br>8. White, off-white stripe, cream, pale yellow, mustard, baby blue, robin's egg blue, dove-gray, navy, and black business shirts<br>9. CUDDLING<br>10. Hate to love<br><br>I devoured this book. <i>Completely devoured it.</i> I was looking for a slow-burn, hate to love office romance, and this was it. I am so happy right now, you guys. I'm literally grinning and giggling as I'm typing this review. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450274768ra/17403686.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once upon a time, in a desperate move to avoid financial ruin, Gamin Publishing and Bexley Books merged companies to form Bexley &amp; Gamin, and <b>Lucy Hutton</b>, the executive assistant to the CEO of Gamin Publishing, ended up sharing her office with <b>Joshua Templeman</b>, the executive assistant to the CEO of Bexley Books. <br><br>The thing about Gamin Publishing and Bexley Books is that they're polar opposites. While Gamin Publishing focuses on the words, Bexley Books focuses on the numbers. Like their home companies, while Lucy handles her job with a smile, Joshua handles his with a frown and a glare. Lucy prefers red lipstick and cute blouses; Joshua has a circuit of identical business shirts in ten different colors. Lucy stands at exactly five feet; Joshua is over six feet tall. Polar opposites.<br><br>For as long as Lucy can remember, she and Joshua have been each other's nemesis. It's their mission to one-up each other. They've been spending their time in the office playing little games to intimidate the other; The Staring Game, The HR Game, The Mirror Game, The Hating Game. The ultimate aim of the games? Make the other smile or cry.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434495937i/15229948.jpg" width="25" height="25”" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <b>
    <i>I'm twenty-eight years old and and it seems I've fallen through the cracks of heaven and hell and into purgatory. A kindergarten classroom."</i>
    <b></b>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The routine all changes when an explosive kiss inside the elevator happens. <br><br>You guyyys! I just love this book. Lucy and Joshua's banters are so witty and funny and damn it, they give as much as the other does. They're two opponents on equal standing, and it was great to see them clash; and even better to see them united. They're just hilarious!<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434495937i/15229948.jpg" width="25" height="25”" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <b>
    <i>So, painting your nails tonight, desperately alone?"<br>"Yes. Masturbating and crying into your pillow tonight, Doctor Josh?"<br>"Yes. And don't call me that."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And the burn is so slow and gradual, I'm pretty sure I was so high-strung by the time the explosion finally happened. I loved it. It was such a long foreplay. I loved watching their relationship change from hate to love. <br><br>I love Joshua! He started off as this arrogant brooding man who would not smile at anything; especially not at anything Lucy says. But as Lucy got to know him, he's not actually that bad. And you know what? He's so much better than Lucy (or I) expected!<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434495937i/15229948.jpg" width="25" height="25”" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <b>
    <i>I haven't wanted you this long, and gone through so much, and given up so much, to have you for one night. It's not enough."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love him. He's so sweet and funny and thoughtful and ugh. He's amazing. AND HE'S A CUDDLER!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472998115ra/20381943.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucy's an extremely kind person who sometimes gets taken advantage of, so it was great to see her stand up for herself. And there was a moment when she was so badass, and I just knew she and Joshua were a perfect pair.<br><br>I'm going to sound like a broken record, but I'm going to say it anyway. I love this book. If you want a light, fluffy, funny, and romantic book, <i>The Hating Game</i> is it. I love it!<br><br><a href="http://ofpensandpages.com" rel="nofollow noopener"> Blog</a> | <a href="http://facebook.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="http://twitter.com/ofpensandpages" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/nissareads" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12618860543148069517" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U5GcRidW6II9NEhoHVFkODyeKTkkHMnleGX89auSzTgoAOVvbr3ZkDYYTyAVgf5aT7W0caG3Fcz7NpXGjMJBQQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('BCzFxI75CZaiRTYh8kmqaIg5PWx/tGH7SRBApvcObLJ/vbztxxI4hKlpMWn6mTAK+xKgJPofvdLKQymV0F7gyw==')})
  }

Worst of all, she’s forcing Olive to spend the day with her sworn enemy, Ethan, who just happens to be the best man.\n\nOlive braces herself to get through 24 hours of wedding hell before she can return to her comfortable, unlucky life.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/18002228.Sally_Thorne">About Sally  Thorne</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>

<a href="/author/show/18002228.Sally_Thorne"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1526286936p3/18002228.jpg);'></div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8563128747327614327">Sally Thorne is the USA Today bestselling author of the office rom-com The Hating Game (2016). It is her debut novel that has sold in over twenty-five countries and is being made into a major motion picture, to be directed by Romy and Michelle’s High School Reunion and The Simpsons Movie director David Mirkin. It was named in the top 20 romance novels of 2016 by the Washington Post and was a top t</span>
  <span id="freeText8563128747327614327" style="display:none">Sally Thorne is the USA Today bestselling author of the office rom-com The Hating Game (2016). It is her debut novel that has sold in over twenty-five countries and is being made into a major motion picture, to be directed by Romy and Michelle’s High School Reunion and The Simpsons Movie director David Mirkin. It was named in the top 20 romance novels of 2016 by the Washington Post and was a top ten finalist in the Goodreads Choice Awards romance category. The Hating Game has been cited as a book that has reinvigorated the romantic comedy genre.<br /><br />Sally’s much anticipated second novel, 99 Percent Mine, was released on 29 January 2019 by William Morrow Books and debuted at #37 on the USA Today Bestseller List. <br /><br />Sally is writing two more books for William Morrow, and is currently drafting her third book. <br /><br />Sally lives in Canberra, Australia, with her husband Roland- plus a pug called Delia and a horse called Louie. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8563128747327614327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
